# <a name="dimensions-and-measurements-available-in-call-quality-dashboard-cqd"></a><span data-ttu-id="ff730-103">在通話品質儀表板和 CQD (中) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-103">Dimensions and measurements available in Call Quality Dashboard (CQD)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ff730-104">電話品質儀表板 (CQD) Microsoft Teams 商務用 Skype可讓您進一商務用 Skype瞭解使用這些服務撥打的通話品質。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-104">The Call Quality Dashboard (CQD) for Microsoft Teams and Skype for Business Online allows you to better understand call quality of calls made with these services.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ff730-105">本主題提供有關透過 CQD 顯示之維度和度量的詳細資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-105">This topic provides detailed information about the dimensions and measurements visible through CQD.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ff730-106">若要深入瞭解 CQD，請參閱使用[CQD](quality-of-experience-review-guide.md)在 Microsoft Teams。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-106">To learn more about CQD, see [Use CQD to manage call and meeting quality in Microsoft Teams](quality-of-experience-review-guide.md).</span></span>

## <a name="first-and-second-endpoint-classification"></a><span data-ttu-id="ff730-107">第一個和第二個端點分類</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-107">First and Second endpoint classification</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ff730-108">CQD 中的許多維度和度量單位會標示為第一個或第二個。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-108">Many of the dimensions and measurements in CQD are labeled as first or second.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ff730-109">下列邏輯會決定串流或通話中涉及的端點會標示為第一個：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-109">The following logic determines which endpoint involved in the stream or call is labeled as first:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="ff730-110">當伺服器 (串流或通話時) 視需要先使用 AV 微控制器、中繼伺服器等伺服器端點。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-110">A Server endpoint (AV MCU, Mediation Server, and so on) is considered First when a Server is involved in the stream or call.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="ff730-111">除非串流位於兩個 Server 端點之間，否則用戶端端點會視為第二個。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-111">A Client endpoint is considered Second unless the stream is between two Server endpoints.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="ff730-112">如果兩個端點類型相同，則根據使用者代理程式類別的內部順序來設定第一個和第二個端點，以確保順序一致。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-112">If both endpoints are the same type, first vs. second is set based on internal ordering of the user agent category to ensure that the ordering is consistent.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ff730-113">例如，這裡的每一列代表串流中涉及的一組使用者代理程式：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-113">For example, here each row represents a pair of User Agents involved in a stream:</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="ff730-114">來電者的使用者代理類別</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-114">User Agent Category of Caller</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="ff730-115">受叫者的使用者代理人類別</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-115">User Agent Category of Callee</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="ff730-116">第一個端點</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-116">First Endpoint</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="ff730-117">第二個端點</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-117">Second Endpoint</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="ff730-118">第一個是來電者</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-118">First Is Caller</span></span>
|:--- |:--- |:--- |:--- |:--- |
|<span data-ttu-id="ff730-119">AV-微控制器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-119">AV-MCU</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="ff730-120">OC (商務用 Skype用戶端) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-120">OC (Skype for Business client)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="ff730-121">AV-微控制器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-121">AV-MCU</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="ff730-122">OC (商務用 Skype用戶端) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-122">OC (Skype for Business client)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="ff730-123">真</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-123">TRUE</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="ff730-124">OC (商務用 Skype用戶端) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-124">OC (Skype for Business client)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="ff730-125">AV-微控制器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-125">AV-MCU</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="ff730-126">AV-微控制器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-126">AV-MCU</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="ff730-127">OC (商務用 Skype用戶端) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-127">OC (Skype for Business client)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="ff730-128">假</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-128">FALSE</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="ff730-129">OC (商務用 Skype用戶端) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-129">OC (Skype for Business client)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="ff730-130">OC (商務用 Skype用戶端) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-130">OC (Skype for Business client)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="ff730-131">OC (商務用 Skype用戶端) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-131">OC (Skype for Business client)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="ff730-132">OC (商務用 Skype用戶端) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-132">OC (Skype for Business client)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="ff730-133">假</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-133">FALSE</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="ff730-134">AV-微控制器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-134">AV-MCU</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="ff730-135">中繼伺服器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-135">Mediation Server</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="ff730-136">中繼伺服器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-136">Mediation Server</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="ff730-137">AV-微控制器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-137">AV-MCU</span></span> ||
|<span data-ttu-id="ff730-138">中繼伺服器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-138">Mediation Server</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="ff730-139">AV-微控制器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-139">AV-MCU</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="ff730-140">中繼伺服器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-140">Mediation Server</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="ff730-141">AV-微控制器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-141">AV-MCU</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="ff730-142">真</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-142">TRUE</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="ff730-143">OC (商務用 Skype用戶端) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-143">OC (Skype for Business client)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="ff730-144">OC 電話 (商務用 Skype IP 電話) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-144">OC Phone (Skype for Business IP Phone)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="ff730-145">OC (商務用 Skype用戶端) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-145">OC (Skype for Business client)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="ff730-146">OC 電話 (商務用 Skype IP 電話) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-146">OC Phone (Skype for Business IP Phone)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="ff730-147">真</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-147">TRUE</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="ff730-148">OC 電話 (商務用 Skype IP 電話) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-148">OC Phone (Skype for Business IP Phone)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="ff730-149">OC (商務用 Skype用戶端) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-149">OC (Skype for Business client)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="ff730-150">OC (商務用 Skype用戶端) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-150">OC (Skype for Business client)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="ff730-151">OC 電話 (商務用 Skype IP 電話) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-151">OC Phone (Skype for Business IP Phone)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="ff730-152">假</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-152">FALSE</span></span> |

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="ff730-153">第一個和第二個分類與呼叫者或來電者端點是分開的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-153">That First and Second classification is separate from which endpoint is the caller or callee.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ff730-154">第一個呼叫者維度可用來協助識別哪個端點是來電者或來電者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-154">The First Is Caller dimension can be used to help identify which endpoint was the caller or callee.</span></span>

## <a name="dimensions"></a><span data-ttu-id="ff730-155">尺寸</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-155">Dimensions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ff730-156">維度資訊部分取決於上傳到 CQD 入口網站的資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-156">Dimensions information is based in part on data uploaded to the CQD portal.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ff730-157">許多維度值也可以做為篩選。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-157">Many Dimension values can also be used as filters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ff730-158">下表列出 CQD 中目前可用的維度，以查詢編輯器中用來建立報表或編輯先前定義的報表的順序列出。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-158">The following table lists the dimensions currently available in CQD, in the order listed in the Query Editor used to create reports or edit previously defined reports.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="ff730-164">第一個 CPU 名稱</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-164">First CPU Name</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="ff730-165">String</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-165">String</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="ff730-166">第一個端點所使用的 CPU 名稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-166">Name of the CPU used by the first endpoint.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="ff730-167">**範例值：** Contoso CPU X11 @ 1.80 GHz</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-167">**Example value:** Contoso CPU X11 @ 1.80 GHz</span></span> | <br/><span data-ttu-id="ff730-168">&bull; 端點未報告此資料</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-168">&bull; This data was not reported by the endpoint</span></span>   |

表示無法建立通話的媒體路徑，但無法分類根本原因。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2288">**Other** - indicates the media path for the call could not be established but the root cause could not be classified.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="ff730-2289">非媒體失敗 - 表示在建立媒體路徑時未偵測到問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2289">Not Media Failure - indicates no issue was detected with the establishment of the media path.</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="ff730-2290">&bull; 由於未知的媒體問題，通話設定失敗</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2290">&bull; Call set up failed due to an unknown media issue</span></span>  |

| <span data-ttu-id="ff730-2567">建立名稱對</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2567">Building Name Pair</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="ff730-2568">列舉的配對</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2568">Enumerated pair</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="ff730-2569">第一個端點和第二個端點的建築物名稱配對。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2569">Pair of the building name for the first and second endpoint.</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="ff730-2570">&bull; 無法確定端點的建築物名稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2570">&bull; The building name for an endpoint could not be determined.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ff730-2571">這可能是因為端點位於公司網路外部，或是從沒有子網映射的網站存取網路。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2571">This could be because the endpoint is located outside the corporate network, or is accessing the network from a site without a subnet mapping.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="ff730-2572">**範例值：** 主樓：分支網站大樓</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2572">**Example value:** Main Building : Branch Site Building</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="ff730-2573">內部公司配對</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2573">Inside Corp Pair</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="ff730-2574">列舉的配對</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2574">Enumerated pair</span></span> <br/><span data-ttu-id="ff730-2575">**可能的值：**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2575">**Possible values:**</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="ff730-2576">內部：內部</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2576">Inside : Inside</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="ff730-2577">內部：外部</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2577">Inside : Outside</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="ff730-2578">外部 ：外部</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2578">Outside : Outside</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ff730-2579">根據子網映射，顯示端點位於公司網路內部或外部的配對。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2579">Pair showing if the endpoints were located inside or outside the corporate network based on the subnet mapping.</span></span>   |   |
| <span data-ttu-id="ff730-2580">案例配對</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2580">Scenario Pair</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="ff730-2581">列舉的配對</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2581">Enumerated pair</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="ff730-2582">根據子網映射和網路連接詳細資料，顯示端點是否位於公司網路內部或外部的配對。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2582">Pair showing if the endpoints were located inside or outside the corporate network based on the subnet mapping and the network connection detail.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="ff730-2583">**注意：** 配對會以 '--' 分隔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2583">**Note:** The pairs are separated by '--'.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="ff730-2584">**範例值：** Client-Inside--Client-Inside-wifi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2584">**Example value:** Client-Inside--Client-Inside-wifi</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="ff730-2585">&bull; 任一端點或兩個端點的網路連接類型不明。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2585">&bull; The network connectivity type was unknown for either or both endpoints.</span></span>  |
||||


### <a name="notes-on-dimension-data-typeunits"></a><span data-ttu-id="ff730-2586">維度資料類型/單位的附注</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2586">Notes on dimension data type/units</span></span>

#### <a name="boolean"></a><span data-ttu-id="ff730-2587">Boolean</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2587">Boolean</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ff730-2588">布林值一直是 True 或 False。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2588">Boolean values are always either True or False.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ff730-2589">在某些情況下，True 也可以表示為 1，而 False 可以表示為 0。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2589">In some cases, True can also be represented as 1 and False can be represented as 0.</span></span>

#### <a name="range"></a><span data-ttu-id="ff730-2590">範圍</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2590">Range</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ff730-2591">提供為範圍或值群組的維度會使用下列格式顯示：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2591">Dimensions that are provided as range or group of values are shown using the following format:</span></span>

 <span data-ttu-id="ff730-2592">_\<sort order string\> [\<lower bound inclusive\> - \<upper bound exclusive\>_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2592">_\<sort order string\> [\<lower bound inclusive\> - \<upper bound exclusive\>_</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ff730-2593">例如， (分鐘) 維度代表通話持續時間，以碼錶示，而值會以值範圍報告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2593">For example, the Duration (Minutes) dimension represents the call duration in seconds with the value reported as a range of values.</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="ff730-2594">持續時間 (分鐘) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2594">Duration (Minutes)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="ff730-2595">如何解譯</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2595">How to interpret</span></span> |
|:--- |:--- |
|<span data-ttu-id="ff730-2596">062：[0 - 0) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2596">062: [0 - 0)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="ff730-2597">串流持續時間 = 0 分鐘</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2597">Stream duration = 0 minutes</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="ff730-2598">064：[1 - 2) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2598">064: [1 - 2)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="ff730-2599">1 分鐘< = < 2 分鐘</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2599">1 minute < = stream duration < 2 minutes</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="ff730-2600">065：[2 - 3) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2600">065: [2 - 3)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="ff730-2601">2 分鐘 < = < 3 分鐘</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2601">2 minutes < = stream duration < 3 minutes</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="ff730-2602">066：[3 到 4) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2602">066: [3–4)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="ff730-2603">3 分鐘< = < 4 分鐘</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2603">3 minutes < = stream duration < 4 minutes</span></span> |
|  | |

<span data-ttu-id="ff730-2604">用來在呈現資料時控制排序次序， \<sort order string> 並可用於篩選。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2604">The \<sort order string> is used to control the sort order when presenting the data and can be used for filtering.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ff730-2605">例如，在持續時間 (分鐘) < "065" 上的篩選會顯示持續時間小於 2 分鐘的資料流程 (因此篩選需要前導的 "0" 才能如預期) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2605">For example, a filter on Duration (Minutes) < "065", would show streams with duration less than 2 minutes (The leading '0' is needed for the filter to work as expected).</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="ff730-2606">排序次序字串的實際值沒有意義。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2606">The actual value of the sort order string isn't significant.</span></span>

#### <a name="enumeration-strings"></a><span data-ttu-id="ff730-2607">列舉字串</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2607">Enumeration strings</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ff730-2608">CQD 所使用的字串通常是從資料檔案衍生，而且這些字串可以是允許長度內幾乎任何字元組合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2608">Strings used by CQD are often derived from data files, and these can be nearly any combination of character within the allowed length.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ff730-2609">某些維度看起來像字串，但因為它們只能是預先定義值的簡短清單之一，因此它們是列舉，而不是真正的字串。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2609">Some dimensions look like strings, but since they can only be one of a short list of predefined values, they are enumerations and not true strings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ff730-2610">某些列舉字串也會成對使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2610">Some enumerations strings are also used in pairs.</span></span>

#### <a name="enumeration-pair"></a><span data-ttu-id="ff730-2611">列舉組</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2611">Enumeration pair</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ff730-2612">提供為列舉對的維度會使用下列格式顯示：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2612">Dimensions that are provided as an enumeration pair are shown using the following format:</span></span>

 <span data-ttu-id="ff730-2613">_\<enumeration value from one end point\> : \<enumeration value from the other endpoint\>_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2613">_\<enumeration value from one end point\> : \<enumeration value from the other endpoint\>_</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ff730-2614">列舉值的順序是一致的，但無法反映第一或第二個端點的順序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2614">The ordering of the enumeration values is consistent but doesn't reflect ordering of the first or second endpoints.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ff730-2615">例如，網路連接詳細資料組會顯示兩個端點的網路連接詳細資料值：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2615">For example, the Network Connection Detail Pair shows the Network Connection Detail values for the two endpoints:</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="ff730-2616">網路連接詳細資料配對</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2616">Network Connection Detail Pair</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="ff730-2617">如何解譯</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2617">How to interpret</span></span> |
|:--- |:--- |
|<span data-ttu-id="ff730-2618">有線 ：有線</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2618">Wired : Wired</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="ff730-2619">第一個端點和第二個端點都使用有線乙太網路連接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2619">First and second endpoints both used wired ethernet connections.</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="ff730-2620">有線 ：wifi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2620">Wired : wifi</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="ff730-2621">第一個端點使用有線乙太網路Wi-Fi，第二個端點則使用有線乙太網路連接，第一個端點則Wi-Fi連接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2621">First endpoint used wired ethernet connection and second endpoint used Wi-Fi connection, or the second endpoint used wired ethernet connection and first endpoint used Wi-Fi connection.</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="ff730-2622">：wifi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2622">: wifi</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="ff730-2623">第一個端點使用 WiFi 連接，而第二個端點所使用的網路連接不明，或第二個端點使用 WiFi 連接，而第一個端點所使用的網路連接是未知的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2623">First endpoint used a WiFi connection and the network connection used by the second endpoint is unknown, or the second endpoint used a WiFi connection and the network connection used by the first endpoint is unknown.</span></span> |
| | |

#### <a name="blank-values"></a><span data-ttu-id="ff730-2624">空白值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2624">Blank values</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ff730-2625">上表列出維度可能空白的可能原因。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2625">The table above lists possible reasons why a dimension may be blank.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ff730-2626">如果 QoE 記錄可用維度為 False，則許多維度和度量單位都會空白。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2626">Many dimensions and measurements will be blank if the QoE Record Available dimension is false.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ff730-2627">這通常會在通話未成功建立時發生。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2627">This typically occurs when the call wasn't successfully established.</span></span>

## <a name="measurements"></a><span data-ttu-id="ff730-2628">測量</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2628">Measurements</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ff730-2629">許多度量值也可以做為篩選。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2629">Many Measurement values can also be used as filters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ff730-2630">下表列出 CQD 中目前可用的度量單位，以查詢編輯器中列出的順序顯示</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2630">The following table lists the measurements currently available in CQD, shown in the order listed in the Query Editor</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="ff730-2631">量值名稱</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2631">Measure Name</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="ff730-2632">單位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2632">Units</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="ff730-2633">描述</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2633">Description</span></span> |
|:--- |:--- |:--- |
|<span data-ttu-id="ff730-2634">資料流程總數</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2634">Total Stream Count</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="ff730-2635">資料流程數目</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2635">Number of streams</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="ff730-2636">無論媒體類型如何，都會為媒體資料流程編號，包括可能沒有媒體類型的可靠性/診斷資料流程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2636">Number media streams regardless of type of media, including reliability/diagnostics streams that may not have a media type.</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="ff730-2637">CDR 可用資料流程總數</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2637">Total CDR Available Stream Count</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ff730-2638">資料流程數目</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2638">Number of streams</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="ff730-2639">提供可靠性/診斷資訊的媒體流數量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2639">Number of media streams with reliability/diagnostics information available.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ff730-2640">請參閱[在 CDR (通話) 錄製商務用 Skype Server](/skypeforbusiness/manage/health-and-monitoring/call-detail-recording-cdr)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2640">See [Call detail recording (CDR) in Skype for Business Server](/skypeforbusiness/manage/health-and-monitoring/call-detail-recording-cdr)</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="ff730-2641">媒體失敗資料流程總數</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2641">Total Media Failed Stream Count</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="ff730-2642">資料流程數目</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2642">Number of streams</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="ff730-2643">無法建立媒體路徑或無法正常終止的資料流程數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2643">Number of streams where either media path could not be established or did not terminate normally.</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="ff730-2644">總通話設定失敗串流計數</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2644">Total Call Setup Failed Stream Count</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="ff730-2645">資料流程數目</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2645">Number of streams</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="ff730-2646">在通話開始時，端點之間無法建立媒體路徑的資料流程數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2646">Number of streams where media path could not be established between the endpoints at the start of the call.</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="ff730-2647">通話中斷串流總數</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2647">Total Call Dropped Stream Count</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="ff730-2648">資料流程數目</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2648">Number of streams</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="ff730-2649">媒體路徑未正常終止的資料流程數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2649">Number of streams where media path did not terminate normally.</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="ff730-2650">媒體成功串流總數</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2650">Total Media Succeeded Stream Count</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="ff730-2651">資料流程數目</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2651">Number of streams</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="ff730-2652">一般建立及終止媒體路徑的資料流程數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2652">Number of streams where media path was established and terminated normally.</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="ff730-2653">總通話設定成功串流計數</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2653">Total Call Setup Succeeded Stream Count</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="ff730-2654">資料流程數</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2654">number of streams</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="ff730-2655">在通話開始時，端點之間可以建立媒體路徑的資料流程數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-2655">Number of streams where media path could be established between the endpoints at the start of the call.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="ff730-3205">PSTN 外發連接計數</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-3205">PSTN Outbound Connected Count</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ff730-3206">通話次數</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-3206">Number of Calls</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ff730-3207">在所選時間範圍內成功連接的通話總數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-3207">Total outbound successfully connected calls in the selected time range.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ff730-3208">此測量有最多 0.2% 的錯誤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-3208">There is an up to 0.2% error for this measure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ff730-3209">詳細資料請參閱下方的附注。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-3209">See note below for details.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="ff730-3210">PSTN 總分鐘數</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-3210">PSTN Total Minutes</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ff730-3211">分鐘</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-3211">Minutes</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ff730-3212">所選時間範圍內的總分鐘使用量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-3212">Total minute usage in the selected time range.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="ff730-3213">PSTN 內入總分鐘數</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-3213">PSTN Inbound Total Minutes</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ff730-3214">分鐘</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-3214">Minutes</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ff730-3215">所選時間範圍內的總內入分鐘使用量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-3215">Total inbound minute usage in the selected time range.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="ff730-3216">PSTN 外發總分鐘數</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-3216">PSTN Outbound Total Minutes</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ff730-3217">分鐘</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-3217">Minutes</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ff730-3218">所選時間範圍內的總外發分鐘使用量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-3218">Total outbound minute usage in the selected time range.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="ff730-3219">PSTN 使用中使用者計數</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-3219">PSTN Active User Count</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ff730-3220">使用者數目</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-3220">Number of users</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ff730-3221">當天至少撥打一通已連接電話的使用者數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-3221">The number of users who made at least one connected call during that day.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="ff730-3222">PSTN 平均通話持續時間</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-3222">PSTN Average Call Duration</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ff730-3223">分鐘</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-3223">Minutes</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ff730-3224">所選時間範圍內所有已連接通話的平均持續時間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-3224">The average duration of all connected calls in the selected time range.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ff730-3225">一般而言，1：1 PSTN 通話需要 4 到 5 分鐘。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-3225">Normally, a 1:1 PSTN call is four to five minutes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ff730-3226">不過，每家公司的平均值可能會有所不同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-3226">However, this average can differ for each company.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="ff730-3227">PSTN 同時通話總數</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-3227">PSTN Total Inbound Concurrent Call Count</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ff730-3228">通話次數</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-3228">Number of calls</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ff730-3229">一分鐘內同時進行中通話數上限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-3229">Maximum number of simultaneous active inbound calls in a minute.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="ff730-3230">PSTN 總外發並行通話計數</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-3230">PSTN Total Outbound Concurrent Call Count</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ff730-3231">通話次數</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-3231">Number of calls</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ff730-3232">一分鐘內同時進行中外通話數上限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-3232">Maximum number of simultaneous active outbound calls in a minute.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="ff730-3233">P50 延遲</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-3233">P50 Latency</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ff730-3234">毫秒</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-3234">Milliseconds</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ff730-3235">50% 的要求應該比給定的延遲更快。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-3235">50% of the requests should be faster than given latency.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="ff730-3236">P50 抖動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-3236">P50 Jitter</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ff730-3237">毫秒</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-3237">Milliseconds</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ff730-3238">50% 的要求應該比給予的抖動更快。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-3238">50% of the requests should be faster than given Jitter.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="ff730-3239">P50 封包遺失率</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-3239">P50 Packet Loss Rate</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ff730-3240">百分比</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-3240">Percentage</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ff730-3241">50% 的要求應低於所給予的封包遺失率。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-3241">50% of the requests should have lower than the given Packet Loss Rate.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="ff730-3242">PSTN 撥出後撥號延遲</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-3242">PSTN Outgoing Post Dial Delay</span></span>| <span data-ttu-id="ff730-3243">毫秒</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-3243">Milliseconds</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ff730-3244">從撥打號碼到來電者或被叫方聽到響鈴時，外撥通話發生的延遲。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-3244">The delay that occurs on outgoing calls measured from the time a number has been dialed until the caller or called party hears ringing.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="ff730-3245">PSTN 內撥後撥號延遲</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-3245">PSTN Incoming Post Dial Delay</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ff730-3246">毫秒</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-3246">Milliseconds</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ff730-3247">從撥打號碼到來電者或被叫方聽到響鈴之前，來電發生的時間或延遲。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-3247">The time or delay that occurs on incoming calls measured from the time a number has been dialed until the caller or called party hears ringing.</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="ff730-3248">PSTN NER 良好百分比</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-3248">PSTN NER Good Percentage</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ff730-3249">百分比</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-3249">Percentage</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ff730-3250">NER 會測量網路傳遞通話的能力，測量已傳送的通話數與傳送給收件者的通話數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-3250">The NER measures the ability of a network to deliver calls by measuring the number of calls sent versus the number of calls delivered to a recipient.</span></span><br/><span data-ttu-id="ff730-3251">NER = (已接來電 + 使用者忙碌 + 無響鈴 + 終端拒絕檢出）/ 總嘗試通話 x 100。此測量有最多 0.2% 的錯誤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-3251">NER = (Answered calls + User Busy + Ring no Answer + Terminal Reject Seizures）/ Total Attempt Calls x 100.There is an up to 0.2% error for this measure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ff730-3252">詳細資料請參閱下方的附注。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-3252">See note below for details.</span></span>|

### <a name="notes-on-measurements"></a><span data-ttu-id="ff730-3253">度量的注意事項</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-3253">Notes on measurements</span></span>

#### <a name="accuracy-limitations"></a><span data-ttu-id="ff730-3254">精確度限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-3254">Accuracy limitations</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="ff730-3255">特定使用者和通話計數測量仰賴對資料集執行不同的計數運算，以計算計數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-3255">Certain user and call count measurements rely on performing a distinct countif operation on the data set to compute the count.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ff730-3256">根據執行作業的列數，不同 countif 作業目前內生的錯誤多達 0.2%。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-3256">There is currently an up to 0.2% error inherent with the distinct countif operation depending on the number of rows the operation is performed on.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ff730-3257">針對最精確的音量，您應該使用串流計數量詞，因為它們不仰賴這個不同的 countif 運算。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-3257">For the most accurate volume, you should use stream count measures since they do not rely on this distinct countif operation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ff730-3258">篩選以降低資料量可能會減少錯誤，但可能無法排除不同通話和使用者計數中的錯誤來源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-3258">Filtering to reduce the data volume may reduce the error but may not eliminate this source of error in distinct call and user counts.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ff730-3259">有關此限制的資訊，請參閱 [dcount 匯總函數](/azure/data-explorer/kusto/query/dcount-aggfunction)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-3259">More information about this limitation can be found here [dcount aggregate function](/azure/data-explorer/kusto/query/dcount-aggfunction).</span></span>

## <a name="filters"></a><span data-ttu-id="ff730-3260">過濾 器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-3260">Filters</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ff730-3261">許多維度和度量值也可以做為篩選。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-3261">Many Dimension and Measurement values can also be used as filters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ff730-3262">您可以使用查詢中的篩選來排除資訊，方法與選取維度或度量單位以在查詢中新增或包含資訊的方式相同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ff730-3262">You can use filters in your query to eliminate information in the same way you'd select a Dimension or Measurement to add or include information in the query.</span></span>
